remarks:        (65020:ms) do NOT send this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (65021:ms) prepend 1x this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (65022:ms) prepend 2x this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (65023:ms) prepend 3x this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (65030:ms) do NOT send this route to peers with RTT <= ms
remarks:        (65031:ms) prepend 1x this route to peers with RTT <= ms
remarks:        (65032:ms) prepend 2x this route to peers with RTT <= ms
remarks:        (65033:ms) prepend 3x this route to peers with RTT <= ms
remarks:
remarks:        In addition to traditional communities, the ECIX route servers
remarks:        also accept the following Large BGP communities [RFC8092]. Please
remarks:        refer to http://largebgpcommunities.net/ for more information.
remarks:        Note that both 16 bit and 32 bit ASNs are supported.
remarks:
remarks:        Large BGP Communities
remarks:        (9033:65000:ASN) do not announce this route to ASN
remarks:        (9033:65000:0) do not announce this route to any ASN
remarks:        (9033:64960:ASN) do announce this route to ASN if (65000:0) is set
remarks:
remarks:        (9033:65001:0) prepend peer AS 1 time to all
remarks:        (9033:65001:ASN) prepend peer AS 1 time to ASN
remarks:        (9033:65002:0) prepend peer AS 2 times to all
remarks:        (9033:65002:ASN) prepend peer AS 2 times to ASN
remarks:        (9033:65003:0) prepend peer AS 3 times to all
remarks:        (9033:65003:ASN) prepend peer AS 3 times to ASN
remarks:
remarks:        (9033:65020:ms) do NOT send this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (9033:65021:ms) prepend 1x this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (9033:65022:ms) prepend 2x this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (9033:65023:ms) prepend 3x this route to peers with RTT >= ms
remarks:        (9033:65030:ms) do NOT send this route to peers with RTT <= ms
remarks:        (9033:65031:ms) prepend 1x this route to peers with RTT <= ms
remarks:        (9033:65032:ms) prepend 2x this route to peers with RTT <= ms
